<span data-ttu-id="a9118-1594">Un `operator++` ou `operator--` implémentation peut être appelée à l’aide de la notation de préfixe ou de suffixe.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1594">An `operator++` or `operator--` implementation can be invoked using either postfix or prefix notation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1595">Il n’est pas possible d’avoir des implémentations d’opérateurs distincts pour les deux notations.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1595">It is not possible to have separate operator implementations for the two notations.</span></span>

### <a name="cast-expressions"></a><span data-ttu-id="a9118-1596">Expressions de cast</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1596">Cast expressions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a9118-1597">Un *cast_expression* est utilisé pour convertir explicitement une expression en un type donné.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1597">A *cast_expression* is used to explicitly convert an expression to a given type.</span></span>

```antlr
cast_expression
    : '(' type ')' unary_expression
    ;
```

<span data-ttu-id="a9118-1598">Un *cast_expression* du formulaire `(T)E`, où `T` est un *type* et `E` est un *unary_expression*, effectue une explicite conversion ([conversions explicites](conversions.md#explicit-conversions)) de la valeur de `E` à taper `T`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1598">A *cast_expression* of the form `(T)E`, where `T` is a *type* and `E` is a *unary_expression*, performs an explicit conversion ([Explicit conversions](conversions.md#explicit-conversions)) of the value of `E` to type `T`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1599">Si aucune conversion explicite `E` à `T`, se produit une erreur au moment de la liaison.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1599">If no explicit conversion exists from `E` to `T`, a binding-time error occurs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1600">Sinon, le résultat est la valeur produite par la conversion explicite.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1600">Otherwise, the result is the value produced by the explicit conversion.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1601">Le résultat est toujours classifié en tant que valeur, même si `E` désigne une variable.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1601">The result is always classified as a value, even if `E` denotes a variable.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a9118-1602">La grammaire d’un *cast_expression* donne lieu à certaines ambiguïtés syntaxiques.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1602">The grammar for a *cast_expression* leads to certain syntactic ambiguities.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1603">Par exemple, l’expression `(x)-y` peut soit être interprétée comme un *cast_expression* (un cast de `-y` vers le type `x`) ou en tant qu’un *additive_expression* combiné avec un *parenthesized_expression* (qui calcule la valeur `x - y)`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1603">For example, the expression `(x)-y` could either be interpreted as a *cast_expression* (a cast of `-y` to type `x`) or as an *additive_expression* combined with a *parenthesized_expression* (which computes the value `x - y)`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a9118-1604">Pour résoudre *cast_expression* ambiguïtés, la règle suivante existe : Une séquence d’un ou plusieurs *jeton*s ([espace blanc](lexical-structure.md#white-space)) placé entre parenthèses est considéré comme le début d’un *cast_expression* uniquement si au moins une des opérations suivantes est remplie :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1604">To resolve *cast_expression* ambiguities, the following rule exists: A sequence of one or more *token*s ([White space](lexical-structure.md#white-space)) enclosed in parentheses is considered the start of a *cast_expression* only if at least one of the following are true:</span></span>

*  <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1605">La séquence de jetons est la grammaire correcte pour un *type*, mais pas pour un *expression*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1605">The sequence of tokens is correct grammar for a *type*, but not for an *expression*.</span></span>
*  <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1606">La séquence de jetons est la grammaire correcte pour un *type*, et le jeton qui suit immédiatement la parenthèse fermante est le jeton «`~`», le jeton «`!`», le jeton «`(`», un  *identificateur* ([séquences d’échappement de caractère Unicode](lexical-structure.md#unicode-character-escape-sequences)), un *littéral* ([littéraux](lexical-structure.md#literals)), ou n’importe quel *mot clé*([Mots clés](lexical-structure.md#keywords)) à l’exception `as` et `is`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1606">The sequence of tokens is correct grammar for a *type*, and the token immediately following the closing parentheses is the token "`~`", the token "`!`", the token "`(`", an *identifier* ([Unicode character escape sequences](lexical-structure.md#unicode-character-escape-sequences)), a *literal* ([Literals](lexical-structure.md#literals)), or any *keyword* ([Keywords](lexical-structure.md#keywords)) except `as` and `is`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a9118-1607">Le terme « grammaire correcte » ci-dessus indique seulement que la séquence de jetons doit être conforme à la production grammaticale particulière.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1607">The term "correct grammar" above means only that the sequence of tokens must conform to the particular grammatical production.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1608">Plus précisément, il ne considère pas la signification réelle de tous les identificateurs qui le composent.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1608">It specifically does not consider the actual meaning of any constituent identifiers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1609">Par exemple, si `x` et `y` sont des identificateurs, puis `x.y` est la grammaire correcte pour un type, même si `x.y` ne désigne en réalité un type.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1609">For example, if `x` and `y` are identifiers, then `x.y` is correct grammar for a type, even if `x.y` doesn't actually denote a type.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a9118-1610">À partir de la règle de suppression qui, si `x` et `y` sont des identificateurs, `(x)y`, `(x)(y)`, et `(x)(-y)` sont *cast_expression*s, mais `(x)-y` n’est pas, même si `x` identifie un type.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1610">From the disambiguation rule it follows that, if `x` and `y` are identifiers, `(x)y`, `(x)(y)`, and `(x)(-y)` are *cast_expression*s, but `(x)-y` is not, even if `x` identifies a type.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1611">Toutefois, si `x` est un mot clé qui identifie un type prédéfini (tel que `int`), puis les quatre formes sont *cast_expression*s (car un tel mot clé ne peut pas être une expression en lui-même).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1611">However, if `x` is a keyword that identifies a predefined type (such as `int`), then all four forms are *cast_expression*s (because such a keyword could not possibly be an expression by itself).</span></span>

### <a name="await-expressions"></a><span data-ttu-id="a9118-1612">Expressions await</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1612">Await expressions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a9118-1613">L’opérateur await est utilisé pour suspendre l’évaluation de la fonction async englobante jusqu'à ce que l’opération asynchrone représentée par l’opérande est terminée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1613">The await operator is used to suspend evaluation of the enclosing async function until the asynchronous operation represented by the operand has completed.</span></span>

```antlr
await_expression
    : 'await' unary_expression
    ;
```

<span data-ttu-id="a9118-1614">Un *await_expression* est autorisée uniquement dans le corps d’une fonction asynchrone ([itérateurs](classes.md#iterators)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1614">An *await_expression* is only allowed in the body of an async function ([Iterators](classes.md#iterators)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1615">Dans l’englobante la plus proche fonction asynchrone, un *await_expression* ne peut pas se produire dans ces emplacements :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1615">Within the nearest enclosing async function, an *await_expression* may not occur in these places:</span></span>

*  <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1616">À l’intérieur d’une fonction anonyme imbriquées (non asynchrone)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1616">Inside a nested (non-async) anonymous function</span></span>
*  <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1617">Dans le bloc d’un *lock_statement*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1617">Inside the block of a *lock_statement*</span></span>
*  <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1618">Dans un contexte unsafe</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1618">In an unsafe context</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a9118-1619">Notez qu’un *await_expression* ne peut pas apparaître à la plupart des emplacements au sein d’un *query_expression*, car celles sont syntaxiquement transformés pour utiliser des expressions lambda non asynchrone.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1619">Note that an *await_expression* cannot occur in most places within a *query_expression*, because those are syntactically transformed to use non-async lambda expressions.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a9118-1620">À l’intérieur d’une fonction async, `await` ne peut pas être utilisé en tant qu’identificateur.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1620">Inside of an async function, `await` cannot be used as an identifier.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1621">Par conséquent, il n’existe aucune ambiguïté syntaxique entre diverses expressions impliquant des identificateurs et les expressions await.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1621">There is therefore no syntactic ambiguity between await-expressions and various expressions involving identifiers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1622">En dehors des fonctions asynchrones, `await` agit comme un identificateur normal.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1622">Outside of async functions, `await` acts as a normal identifier.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a9118-1623">L’opérande d’un *await_expression* est appelé le ***tâche***.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1623">The operand of an *await_expression* is called the ***task***.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1624">Il représente une opération asynchrone qui peut être ou non complète au moment où le *await_expression* est évaluée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1624">It represents an asynchronous operation that may or may not be complete at the time the *await_expression* is evaluated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1625">L’objectif de l’opérateur await est pour suspendre l’exécution de la fonction async englobante jusqu'à ce que la tâche attendue soit terminée et pour obtenir son résultat.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1625">The purpose of the await operator is to suspend execution of the enclosing async function until the awaited task is complete, and then obtain its outcome.</span></span>

#### <a name="awaitable-expressions"></a><span data-ttu-id="a9118-1626">Expressions await</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1626">Awaitable expressions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a9118-1627">La tâche d’une expression await est nécessaire pour être ***awaitable***.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1627">The task of an await expression is required to be ***awaitable***.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1628">Une expression `t` peut être attendu si dont l’un des éléments suivants :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1628">An expression `t` is awaitable if one of the following holds:</span></span>

*  <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1629">`t` est de type au moment de compilation `dynamic`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1629">`t` is of compile time type `dynamic`</span></span>
*  <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1630">`t` a une méthode d’extension ou d’instance accessible appelée `GetAwaiter` sans paramètres et aucun paramètre de type et un type de retour `A` pour lequel toutes les conditions suivantes contiennent :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1630">`t` has an accessible instance or extension method called `GetAwaiter` with no parameters and no type parameters, and a return type `A` for which all of the following hold:</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1631">`A` implémente l’interface `System.Runtime.CompilerServices.INotifyCompletion` (ci-après appelée `INotifyCompletion` par souci de concision)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1631">`A` implements the interface `System.Runtime.CompilerServices.INotifyCompletion` (hereafter known as `INotifyCompletion` for brevity)</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1632">`A` a une propriété d’instance accessible et lisible `IsCompleted` de type `bool`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1632">`A` has an accessible, readable instance property `IsCompleted` of type `bool`</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1633">`A` a une méthode d’instance accessible `GetResult` sans paramètres et aucun paramètre de type</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1633">`A` has an accessible instance method `GetResult` with no parameters and no type parameters</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a9118-1634">L’objectif de la `GetAwaiter` méthode consiste à obtenir un ***awaiter*** pour la tâche.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1634">The purpose of the `GetAwaiter` method is to obtain an ***awaiter*** for the task.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1635">Le type `A` est appelé le ***type d’entité awaiter*** pour l’expression await.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1635">The type `A` is called the ***awaiter type*** for the await expression.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a9118-1636">L’objectif de la `IsCompleted` propriété consiste à déterminer si la tâche est déjà terminée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1636">The purpose of the `IsCompleted` property is to determine if the task is already complete.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1637">Dans ce cas, il n’est pas nécessaire de suspendre l’évaluation.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1637">If so, there is no need to suspend evaluation.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a9118-1638">L’objectif de la `INotifyCompletion.OnCompleted` méthode consiste à créer une « continuation » à la tâche ; par exemple, un délégué (de type `System.Action`) qui sera appelé une fois que la tâche est terminée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1638">The purpose of the `INotifyCompletion.OnCompleted` method is to sign up a "continuation" to the task; i.e. a delegate (of type `System.Action`) that will be invoked once the task is complete.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a9118-1639">L’objectif de la `GetResult` méthode consiste à obtenir le résultat de la tâche une fois celle-ci terminée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1639">The purpose of the `GetResult` method is to obtain the outcome of the task once it is complete.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1640">Ce résultat peut être réussite, éventuellement avec une valeur de résultat, ou il peut être une exception qui est levée par le `GetResult` (méthode).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1640">This outcome may be successful completion, possibly with a result value, or it may be an exception which is thrown by the `GetResult` method.</span></span>

#### <a name="classification-of-await-expressions"></a><span data-ttu-id="a9118-1641">Classification des expressions await</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1641">Classification of await expressions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a9118-1642">L’expression `await t` est classé de la même façon que l’expression `(t).GetAwaiter().GetResult()`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1642">The expression `await t` is classified the same way as the expression `(t).GetAwaiter().GetResult()`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1643">Par conséquent, si le type de retour de `GetResult` est `void`, le *await_expression* est classé comme rien.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1643">Thus, if the return type of `GetResult` is `void`, the *await_expression* is classified as nothing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1644">S’il a un type de retour non void `T`, le *await_expression* est classé en tant que valeur de type `T`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1644">If it has a non-void return type `T`, the *await_expression* is classified as a value of type `T`.</span></span>

#### <a name="runtime-evaluation-of-await-expressions"></a><span data-ttu-id="a9118-1645">Évaluation de runtime des expressions await</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1645">Runtime evaluation of await expressions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a9118-1646">Lors de l’exécution, l’expression `await t` est évaluée comme suit :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1646">At runtime, the expression `await t` is evaluated as follows:</span></span>

*  <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1647">Un élément awaiter `a` est obtenue en évaluant l’expression `(t).GetAwaiter()`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1647">An awaiter `a` is obtained by evaluating the expression `(t).GetAwaiter()`.</span></span>
*  <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1648">Un `bool` `b` est obtenue en évaluant l’expression `(a).IsCompleted`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1648">A `bool` `b` is obtained by evaluating the expression `(a).IsCompleted`.</span></span>
*  <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1649">Si `b` est `false` puis évaluation varie selon que `a` implémente l’interface `System.Runtime.CompilerServices.ICriticalNotifyCompletion` (ci-après appelée `ICriticalNotifyCompletion` par souci de concision).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1649">If `b` is `false` then evaluation depends on whether `a` implements the interface `System.Runtime.CompilerServices.ICriticalNotifyCompletion` (hereafter known as `ICriticalNotifyCompletion` for brevity).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1650">Cette vérification est effectuée lors de la liaison de temps ; par exemple, lors de l’exécution si `a` a le type de temps de compilation `dynamic`et au moment de la compilation dans le cas contraire.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1650">This check is done at binding time; i.e. at runtime if `a` has the compile time type `dynamic`, and at compile time otherwise.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1651">Laisser `r` désignent le délégué de reprise ([itérateurs](classes.md#iterators)) :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1651">Let `r` denote the resumption delegate ([Iterators](classes.md#iterators)):</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1652">Si `a` n’implémente pas `ICriticalNotifyCompletion`, puis l’expression `(a as (INotifyCompletion)).OnCompleted(r)` est évaluée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1652">If `a` does not implement `ICriticalNotifyCompletion`, then the expression `(a as (INotifyCompletion)).OnCompleted(r)` is evaluated.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1653">Si `a` implémente `ICriticalNotifyCompletion`, puis l’expression `(a as (ICriticalNotifyCompletion)).UnsafeOnCompleted(r)` est évaluée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1653">If `a` does implement `ICriticalNotifyCompletion`, then the expression `(a as (ICriticalNotifyCompletion)).UnsafeOnCompleted(r)` is evaluated.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1654">Version d’évaluation est interrompue puis et contrôle est retourné à l’appelant actuel de la fonction async.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1654">Evaluation is then suspended, and control is returned to the current caller of the async function.</span></span>
*  <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1655">Soit immédiatement après (si `b` a été `true`), ou en cas d’un appel ultérieur du délégué de reprise (si `b` a été `false`), l’expression `(a).GetResult()` est évaluée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1655">Either immediately after (if `b` was `true`), or upon later invocation of the resumption delegate (if `b` was `false`), the expression `(a).GetResult()` is evaluated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1656">Si elle retourne une valeur, cette valeur est le résultat de la *await_expression*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1656">If it returns a value, that value is the result of the *await_expression*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1657">Sinon, le résultat est nothing.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1657">Otherwise the result is nothing.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a9118-1658">Implémentation d’un élément awaiter méthodes d’interface `INotifyCompletion.OnCompleted` et `ICriticalNotifyCompletion.UnsafeOnCompleted` doit provoquer le délégué `r` à appeler au maximum une fois.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1658">An awaiter's implementation of the interface methods `INotifyCompletion.OnCompleted` and `ICriticalNotifyCompletion.UnsafeOnCompleted` should cause the delegate `r` to be invoked at most once.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1659">Sinon, le comportement de la fonction async englobante est indéfini.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1659">Otherwise, the behavior of the enclosing async function is undefined.</span></span>

## <a name="arithmetic-operators"></a><span data-ttu-id="a9118-1660">Opérateurs arithmétiques</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1660">Arithmetic operators</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a9118-1661">Le `*`, `/`, `%`, `+`, et `-` sont appelés les opérateurs arithmétiques.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1661">The `*`, `/`, `%`, `+`, and `-` operators are called the arithmetic operators.</span></span>

```antlr
multiplicative_expression
    : unary_expression
    | multiplicative_expression '*' unary_expression
    | multiplicative_expression '/' unary_expression
    | multiplicative_expression '%' unary_expression
    ;

additive_expression
    : multiplicative_expression
    | additive_expression '+' multiplicative_expression
    | additive_expression '-' multiplicative_expression
    ;
```

<span data-ttu-id="a9118-1662">Si un opérande d’un opérateur arithmétique a le type de compilation `dynamic`, puis l’expression est liée dynamiquement ([liaison dynamique](expressions.md#dynamic-binding)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1662">If an operand of an arithmetic operator has the compile-time type `dynamic`, then the expression is dynamically bound ([Dynamic binding](expressions.md#dynamic-binding)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1663">Dans ce cas le type de compilation de l’expression est `dynamic`, et la résolution décrite ci-dessous aura lieu au moment de l’exécution à l’aide du type au moment de l’exécution de ces opérandes qui ont le type de compilation `dynamic`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1663">In this case the compile-time type of the expression is `dynamic`, and the resolution described below will take place at run-time using the run-time type of those operands that have the compile-time type `dynamic`.</span></span>

### <a name="multiplication-operator"></a><span data-ttu-id="a9118-1664">Opérateur de multiplication</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1664">Multiplication operator</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a9118-1665">Pour une opération du formulaire `x * y`, opérateur binaire de résolution de surcharge ([opérateur binaire de résolution de surcharge](expressions.md#binary-operator-overload-resolution)) est appliquée pour sélectionner l’implémentation d’un opérateur spécifique.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1665">For an operation of the form `x * y`, binary operator overload resolution ([Binary operator overload resolution](expressions.md#binary-operator-overload-resolution)) is applied to select a specific operator implementation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1666">Les opérandes sont convertis en types de paramètres de l’opérateur sélectionné et le type du résultat est le type de retour de l’opérateur.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1666">The operands are converted to the parameter types of the selected operator, and the type of the result is the return type of the operator.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a9118-1667">Les opérateurs de multiplication prédéfinis sont répertoriés ci-dessous.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1667">The predefined multiplication operators are listed below.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1668">Tous les opérateurs calculent le produit des `x` et `y`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1668">The operators all compute the product of `x` and `y`.</span></span>

*  <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1669">Multiplication d’entiers :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1669">Integer multiplication:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   int operator *(int x, int y);
   uint operator *(uint x, uint y);
   long operator *(long x, long y);
   ulong operator *(ulong x, ulong y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1670">Dans un `checked` contexte, si le produit est en dehors de la plage du type du résultat, un `System.OverflowException` est levée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1670">In a `checked` context, if the product is outside the range of the result type, a `System.OverflowException` is thrown.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1671">Dans un `unchecked` contexte, dépassements de capacité ne sont pas signalés et n’importe quel bits de poids fort significatifs en dehors de la plage du type du résultat sont ignorés.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1671">In an `unchecked` context, overflows are not reported and any significant high-order bits outside the range of the result type are discarded.</span></span>


*  <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1672">Multiplication à virgule flottante :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1672">Floating-point multiplication:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   float operator *(float x, float y);
   double operator *(double x, double y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1673">Le produit est calculé selon les règles de la norme IEEE 754 arithmétique.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1673">The product is computed according to the rules of IEEE 754 arithmetic.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1674">Le tableau suivant répertorie les résultats de toutes les combinaisons possibles de valeurs finies, les zéros non significatifs, les valeurs infinies et NaN.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1674">The following table lists the results of all possible combinations of nonzero finite values, zeros, infinities, and NaN's.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1675">Dans la table, `x` et `y` sont des valeurs finies positives.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1675">In the table, `x` and `y` are positive finite values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1676">`z` est le résultat de `x * y`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1676">`z` is the result of `x * y`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1677">Si le résultat est trop grand pour le type de destination, `z` est l’infini.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1677">If the result is too large for the destination type, `z` is infinity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1678">Si le résultat est trop petit pour le type de destination, `z` est égal à zéro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1678">If the result is too small for the destination type, `z` is zero.</span></span>

   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1702">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1702">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1703">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1703">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1704">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1704">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1705">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1705">+0</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1706">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1706">-0</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1707">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1707">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1708">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1708">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1709">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1709">NaN</span></span> | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1710">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1710">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1711">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1711">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1712">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1712">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1713">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1713">-0</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1714">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1714">+0</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1715">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1715">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1716">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1716">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1717">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1717">NaN</span></span> | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1718">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1718">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1719">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1719">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1720">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1720">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1721">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1721">NaN</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1722">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1722">NaN</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1723">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1723">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1724">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1724">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1725">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1725">NaN</span></span> | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1726">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1726">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1727">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1727">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1728">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1728">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1729">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1729">NaN</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1730">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1730">NaN</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1731">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1731">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1732">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1732">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1733">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1733">NaN</span></span> | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1734">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1734">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1735">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1735">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1736">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1736">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1737">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1737">NaN</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1738">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1738">NaN</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1739">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1739">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1740">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1740">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1741">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1741">NaN</span></span> | 

*  <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1742">Multiplication de nombres décimaux :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1742">Decimal multiplication:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   decimal operator *(decimal x, decimal y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1743">Si la valeur résultante est trop grande pour être représenté dans le `decimal` format, un `System.OverflowException` est levée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1743">If the resulting value is too large to represent in the `decimal` format, a `System.OverflowException` is thrown.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1744">Si la valeur de résultat est trop petite pour être représenté dans le `decimal` format, le résultat est égal à zéro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1744">If the result value is too small to represent in the `decimal` format, the result is zero.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1745">La mise à l’échelle du résultat, avant tout arrondi, est la somme des échelles des deux opérandes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1745">The scale of the result, before any rounding, is the sum of the scales of the two operands.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1746">Multiplication de nombres décimaux est équivalente à l’aide de l’opérateur de multiplication du type `System.Decimal`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1746">Decimal multiplication is equivalent to using the multiplication operator of type `System.Decimal`.</span></span>


### <a name="division-operator"></a><span data-ttu-id="a9118-1747">Opérateur de division</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1747">Division operator</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a9118-1748">Pour une opération du formulaire `x / y`, opérateur binaire de résolution de surcharge ([opérateur binaire de résolution de surcharge](expressions.md#binary-operator-overload-resolution)) est appliquée pour sélectionner l’implémentation d’un opérateur spécifique.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1748">For an operation of the form `x / y`, binary operator overload resolution ([Binary operator overload resolution](expressions.md#binary-operator-overload-resolution)) is applied to select a specific operator implementation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1749">Les opérandes sont convertis en types de paramètres de l’opérateur sélectionné et le type du résultat est le type de retour de l’opérateur.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1749">The operands are converted to the parameter types of the selected operator, and the type of the result is the return type of the operator.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a9118-1750">Les opérateurs de division prédéfinis sont répertoriés ci-dessous.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1750">The predefined division operators are listed below.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1751">Tous les opérateurs calculent le quotient de `x` et `y`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1751">The operators all compute the quotient of `x` and `y`.</span></span>

*  <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1752">Division d’entier :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1752">Integer division:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   int operator /(int x, int y);
   uint operator /(uint x, uint y);
   long operator /(long x, long y);
   ulong operator /(ulong x, ulong y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1753">Si la valeur de l’opérande droite est zéro, un `System.DivideByZeroException` est levée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1753">If the value of the right operand is zero, a `System.DivideByZeroException` is thrown.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1754">La division arrondit le résultat vers zéro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1754">The division rounds the result towards zero.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1755">Par conséquent, la valeur absolue du résultat est le plus grand entier possible qui est inférieur ou égal à la valeur absolue du quotient de deux opérandes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1755">Thus the absolute value of the result is the largest possible integer that is less than or equal to the absolute value of the quotient of the two operands.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1756">Le résultat est zéro ou une valeur positive lorsque les deux opérandes ont le même signe et zéro ou négatif lorsque les deux opérandes ont des signes opposés.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1756">The result is zero or positive when the two operands have the same sign and zero or negative when the two operands have opposite signs.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1757">Si l’opérande gauche est le plus petit qui peut être représenté `int` ou `long` valeur et l’opérande de droite est `-1`, un dépassement de capacité se produit.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1757">If the left operand is the smallest representable `int` or `long` value and the right operand is `-1`, an overflow occurs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1758">Dans un `checked` contexte, cela entraîne un `System.ArithmeticException` (ou une sous-classe) devant être levé.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1758">In a `checked` context, this causes a `System.ArithmeticException` (or a subclass thereof) to be thrown.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1759">Dans un `unchecked` contexte, il est défini par l’implémentation pour savoir si un `System.ArithmeticException` (ou une sous-classe) est levée ou le dépassement de capacité n’est pas rapporté par la valeur obtenue en cours de l’opérande gauche.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1759">In an `unchecked` context, it is implementation-defined as to whether a `System.ArithmeticException` (or a subclass thereof) is thrown or the overflow goes unreported with the resulting value being that of the left operand.</span></span>

*  <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1760">Division à virgule flottante :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1760">Floating-point division:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   float operator /(float x, float y);
   double operator /(double x, double y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1761">Le quotient est calculé selon les règles de la norme IEEE 754 arithmétique.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1761">The quotient is computed according to the rules of IEEE 754 arithmetic.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1762">Le tableau suivant répertorie les résultats de toutes les combinaisons possibles de valeurs finies, les zéros non significatifs, les valeurs infinies et NaN.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1762">The following table lists the results of all possible combinations of nonzero finite values, zeros, infinities, and NaN's.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1763">Dans la table, `x` et `y` sont des valeurs finies positives.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1763">In the table, `x` and `y` are positive finite values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1764">`z` est le résultat de `x / y`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1764">`z` is the result of `x / y`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1765">Si le résultat est trop grand pour le type de destination, `z` est l’infini.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1765">If the result is too large for the destination type, `z` is infinity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1766">Si le résultat est trop petit pour le type de destination, `z` est égal à zéro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1766">If the result is too small for the destination type, `z` is zero.</span></span>

   |      |      |      |      |      |      |      |      |
   |:----:|:----:|:----:|:----:|:----:|:----:|:----:|:----:|

   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1790">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1790">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1791">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1791">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1792">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1792">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1793">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1793">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1794">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1794">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1795">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1795">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1796">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1796">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1797">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1797">NaN</span></span>  | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1798">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1798">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1799">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1799">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1800">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1800">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1801">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1801">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1802">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1802">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1803">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1803">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1804">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1804">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1805">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1805">NaN</span></span>  | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1806">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1806">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1807">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1807">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1808">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1808">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1809">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1809">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1810">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1810">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1811">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1811">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1812">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1812">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1813">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1813">NaN</span></span>  | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1814">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1814">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1815">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1815">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1816">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1816">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1817">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1817">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1818">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1818">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1819">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1819">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1820">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1820">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1821">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1821">NaN</span></span>  | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1822">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1822">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1823">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1823">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1824">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1824">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1825">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1825">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1826">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1826">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1827">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1827">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1828">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1828">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1829">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1829">NaN</span></span>  | 

*  <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1830">Division décimale :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1830">Decimal division:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   decimal operator /(decimal x, decimal y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1831">Si la valeur de l’opérande droite est zéro, un `System.DivideByZeroException` est levée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1831">If the value of the right operand is zero, a `System.DivideByZeroException` is thrown.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1832">Si la valeur résultante est trop grande pour être représenté dans le `decimal` format, un `System.OverflowException` est levée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1832">If the resulting value is too large to represent in the `decimal` format, a `System.OverflowException` is thrown.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1833">Si la valeur de résultat est trop petite pour être représenté dans le `decimal` format, le résultat est égal à zéro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1833">If the result value is too small to represent in the `decimal` format, the result is zero.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1834">La mise à l’échelle du résultat est la plus petite qui conservera un résultat égal à la plus proche de la valeur décimale représentable le résultat mathématique true.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1834">The scale of the result is the smallest scale that will preserve a result equal to the nearest representable decimal value to the true mathematical result.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1835">La division décimale équivaut à l’utilisation de l’opérateur de division du type `System.Decimal`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1835">Decimal division is equivalent to using the division operator of type `System.Decimal`.</span></span>


### <a name="remainder-operator"></a><span data-ttu-id="a9118-1836">Opérateur de reste</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1836">Remainder operator</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a9118-1837">Pour une opération du formulaire `x % y`, opérateur binaire de résolution de surcharge ([opérateur binaire de résolution de surcharge](expressions.md#binary-operator-overload-resolution)) est appliquée pour sélectionner l’implémentation d’un opérateur spécifique.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1837">For an operation of the form `x % y`, binary operator overload resolution ([Binary operator overload resolution](expressions.md#binary-operator-overload-resolution)) is applied to select a specific operator implementation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1838">Les opérandes sont convertis en types de paramètres de l’opérateur sélectionné et le type du résultat est le type de retour de l’opérateur.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1838">The operands are converted to the parameter types of the selected operator, and the type of the result is the return type of the operator.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a9118-1839">Les opérateurs de reste prédéfinis sont répertoriés ci-dessous.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1839">The predefined remainder operators are listed below.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1840">Tous les opérateurs de calcul le reste de la division entre `x` et `y`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1840">The operators all compute the remainder of the division between `x` and `y`.</span></span>

*  <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1841">Reste entier :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1841">Integer remainder:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   int operator %(int x, int y);
   uint operator %(uint x, uint y);
   long operator %(long x, long y);
   ulong operator %(ulong x, ulong y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1842">Le résultat de `x % y` est la valeur produite par `x - (x / y) * y`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1842">The result of `x % y` is the value produced by `x - (x / y) * y`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1843">Si `y` est égal à zéro, un `System.DivideByZeroException` est levée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1843">If `y` is zero, a `System.DivideByZeroException` is thrown.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1844">Si l’opérande gauche est le plus petit `int` ou `long` valeur et l’opérande de droite est `-1`, un `System.OverflowException` est levée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1844">If the left operand is the smallest `int` or `long` value and the right operand is `-1`, a `System.OverflowException` is thrown.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1845">En aucun cas ne `x % y` lever une exception où `x / y` pas lève une exception.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1845">In no case does `x % y` throw an exception where `x / y` would not throw an exception.</span></span>

*  <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1846">Reste à virgule flottante :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1846">Floating-point remainder:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   float operator %(float x, float y);
   double operator %(double x, double y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1847">Le tableau suivant répertorie les résultats de toutes les combinaisons possibles de valeurs finies, les zéros non significatifs, les valeurs infinies et NaN.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1847">The following table lists the results of all possible combinations of nonzero finite values, zeros, infinities, and NaN's.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1848">Dans la table, `x` et `y` sont des valeurs finies positives.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1848">In the table, `x` and `y` are positive finite values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1849">`z` est le résultat de `x % y` et est calculée en tant que `x - n * y`, où `n` est le plus grand entier possible qui est inférieur ou égal à `x / y`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1849">`z` is the result of `x % y` and is computed as `x - n * y`, where `n` is the largest possible integer that is less than or equal to `x / y`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1850">Cette méthode de calcul du reste est analogue à celle utilisée pour les opérandes entiers, mais diffère de la définition de la norme IEEE 754 (dans lequel `n` est l’entier le plus proche `x / y`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1850">This method of computing the remainder is analogous to that used for integer operands, but differs from the IEEE 754 definition (in which `n` is the integer closest to `x / y`).</span></span>

   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1866">-x</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1866">-x</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1867">-z</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1867">-z</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1868">-z</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1868">-z</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1869">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1869">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1870">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1870">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1871">-x</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1871">-x</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1872">-x</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1872">-x</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1873">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1873">NaN</span></span>  | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1874">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1874">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1875">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1875">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1876">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1876">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1877">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1877">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1878">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1878">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1879">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1879">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1880">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1880">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1881">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1881">NaN</span></span>  | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1882">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1882">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1883">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1883">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1884">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1884">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1885">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1885">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1886">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1886">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1887">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1887">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1888">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1888">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1889">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1889">NaN</span></span>  | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1890">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1890">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1891">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1891">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1892">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1892">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1893">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1893">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1894">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1894">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1895">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1895">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1896">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1896">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1897">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1897">NaN</span></span>  | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1898">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1898">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1899">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1899">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1900">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1900">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1901">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1901">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1902">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1902">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1903">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1903">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1904">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1904">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1905">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1905">NaN</span></span>  | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1906">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1906">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1907">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1907">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1908">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1908">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1909">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1909">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1910">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1910">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1911">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1911">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1912">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1912">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1913">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1913">NaN</span></span>  | 

*  <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1914">Reste de nombres décimaux :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1914">Decimal remainder:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   decimal operator %(decimal x, decimal y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1915">Si la valeur de l’opérande droite est zéro, un `System.DivideByZeroException` est levée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1915">If the value of the right operand is zero, a `System.DivideByZeroException` is thrown.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1916">La mise à l’échelle du résultat, avant tout arrondi, est la plus grande des échelles des deux opérandes, et le signe du résultat, si différente de zéro, est identique à celui de `x`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1916">The scale of the result, before any rounding, is the larger of the scales of the two operands, and the sign of the result, if non-zero, is the same as that of `x`.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1917">Reste de nombres décimaux est équivalente à l’aide de l’opérateur de reste du type `System.Decimal`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1917">Decimal remainder is equivalent to using the remainder operator of type `System.Decimal`.</span></span>


### <a name="addition-operator"></a><span data-ttu-id="a9118-1918">Opérateur d’addition</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1918">Addition operator</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a9118-1919">Pour une opération du formulaire `x + y`, opérateur binaire de résolution de surcharge ([opérateur binaire de résolution de surcharge](expressions.md#binary-operator-overload-resolution)) est appliquée pour sélectionner l’implémentation d’un opérateur spécifique.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1919">For an operation of the form `x + y`, binary operator overload resolution ([Binary operator overload resolution](expressions.md#binary-operator-overload-resolution)) is applied to select a specific operator implementation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1920">Les opérandes sont convertis en types de paramètres de l’opérateur sélectionné et le type du résultat est le type de retour de l’opérateur.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1920">The operands are converted to the parameter types of the selected operator, and the type of the result is the return type of the operator.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a9118-1921">Les opérateurs d’addition prédéfinis sont répertoriées ci-dessous.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1921">The predefined addition operators are listed below.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1922">Pour les types numériques et d’énumération, les opérateurs d’addition prédéfinis calculent la somme des deux opérandes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1922">For numeric and enumeration types, the predefined addition operators compute the sum of the two operands.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1923">Lorsqu’un ou deux opérandes sont de type chaîne, les opérateurs d’addition prédéfinis concaténer la représentation sous forme de chaîne des opérandes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1923">When one or both operands are of type string, the predefined addition operators concatenate the string representation of the operands.</span></span>

*  <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1924">Ajout de l’entier :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1924">Integer addition:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   int operator +(int x, int y);
   uint operator +(uint x, uint y);
   long operator +(long x, long y);
   ulong operator +(ulong x, ulong y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1925">Dans un `checked` contexte, si la somme est en dehors de la plage du type du résultat, un `System.OverflowException` est levée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1925">In a `checked` context, if the sum is outside the range of the result type, a `System.OverflowException` is thrown.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1926">Dans un `unchecked` contexte, dépassements de capacité ne sont pas signalés et n’importe quel bits de poids fort significatifs en dehors de la plage du type du résultat sont ignorés.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1926">In an `unchecked` context, overflows are not reported and any significant high-order bits outside the range of the result type are discarded.</span></span>

*  <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1927">Addition à virgule flottante :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1927">Floating-point addition:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   float operator +(float x, float y);
   double operator +(double x, double y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1928">La somme est calculée selon les règles de la norme IEEE 754 arithmétique.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1928">The sum is computed according to the rules of IEEE 754 arithmetic.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1929">Le tableau suivant répertorie les résultats de toutes les combinaisons possibles de valeurs finies, les zéros non significatifs, les valeurs infinies et NaN.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1929">The following table lists the results of all possible combinations of nonzero finite values, zeros, infinities, and NaN's.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1930">Dans la table, `x` et `y` sont des valeurs finies, et `z` est le résultat de `x + y`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1930">In the table, `x` and `y` are nonzero finite values, and `z` is the result of `x + y`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1931">Si `x` et `y` ont la même grandeur, mais l’opposé de signes, `z` est un zéro positif.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1931">If `x` and `y` have the same magnitude but opposite signs, `z` is positive zero.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1932">Si `x + y` est trop grand pour être représenté dans le type de destination, `z` est un infini ayant le même signe que `x + y`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1932">If `x + y` is too large to represent in the destination type, `z` is an infinity with the same sign as `x + y`.</span></span>

   |      |      |      |      |      |      |      |
   |:----:|:----:|:----:|:----:|:----:|:----:|:----:|
   |      | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1933">o</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1933">y</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1934">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1934">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1935">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1935">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1936">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1936">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1937">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1937">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1938">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1938">NaN</span></span>  | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1939">x</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1939">x</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1940">e</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1940">z</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1941">x</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1941">x</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1942">x</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1942">x</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1943">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1943">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1944">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1944">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1945">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1945">NaN</span></span>  | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1946">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1946">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1947">o</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1947">y</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1948">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1948">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1949">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1949">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1950">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1950">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1951">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1951">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1952">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1952">NaN</span></span>  | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1953">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1953">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1954">o</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1954">y</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1955">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1955">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1956">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1956">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1957">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1957">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1958">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1958">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1959">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1959">NaN</span></span>  | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1960">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1960">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1961">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1961">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1962">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1962">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1963">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1963">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1964">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1964">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1965">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1965">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1966">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1966">NaN</span></span>  | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1967">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1967">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1968">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1968">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1969">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1969">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1970">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1970">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1971">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1971">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1972">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1972">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1973">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1973">NaN</span></span>  | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1974">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1974">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1975">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1975">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1976">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1976">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1977">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1977">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1978">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1978">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1979">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1979">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1980">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1980">NaN</span></span>  | 

*  <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1981">Addition de nombres décimaux :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1981">Decimal addition:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   decimal operator +(decimal x, decimal y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1982">Si la valeur résultante est trop grande pour être représenté dans le `decimal` format, un `System.OverflowException` est levée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1982">If the resulting value is too large to represent in the `decimal` format, a `System.OverflowException` is thrown.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1983">L’échelle du résultat, avant tout arrondi, est la plus grande des échelles des deux opérandes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1983">The scale of the result, before any rounding, is the larger of the scales of the two operands.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1984">Addition de nombres décimaux est équivalente à l’aide de l’opérateur d’addition de type `System.Decimal`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1984">Decimal addition is equivalent to using the addition operator of type `System.Decimal`.</span></span>

*  <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1985">Ajout de l’énumération.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1985">Enumeration addition.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1986">Chaque type énumération fournit implicitement suivantes des opérateurs, prédéfinis où `E` est le type enum, et `U` est le type sous-jacent de `E`:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1986">Every enumeration type implicitly provides the following predefined operators, where `E` is the enum type, and `U` is the underlying type of `E`:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   E operator +(E x, U y);
   E operator +(U x, E y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1987">Au moment de l’exécution, ces opérateurs sont évalués exactement comme `(E)((U)x + (U)y)`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1987">At run-time these operators are evaluated exactly as `(E)((U)x + (U)y)`.</span></span>

*  <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1988">Concaténation de chaînes :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1988">String concatenation:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   string operator +(string x, string y);
   string operator +(string x, object y);
   string operator +(object x, string y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1989">Ces surcharges de la ressource binaire `+` opérateur effectuer la concaténation de chaînes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1989">These overloads of the binary `+` operator perform string concatenation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1990">Si un opérande de concaténation de chaînes est `null`, une chaîne vide est substituée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1990">If an operand of string concatenation is `null`, an empty string is substituted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1991">Sinon, n’importe quel argument autre qu’une chaîne est converti en sa représentation de chaîne en appelant virtuel `ToString` méthode héritée du type `object`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1991">Otherwise, any non-string argument is converted to its string representation by invoking the virtual `ToString` method inherited from type `object`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1992">Si `ToString` retourne `null`, une chaîne vide est substituée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1992">If `ToString` returns `null`, an empty string is substituted.</span></span>

   ```csharp
   using System;
   
   class Test
   {
       static void Main() {
           string s = null;
           Console.WriteLine("s = >" + s + "<");        // displays s = ><
           int i = 1;
           Console.WriteLine("i = " + i);               // displays i = 1
           float f = 1.2300E+15F;
           Console.WriteLine("f = " + f);               // displays f = 1.23E+15
           decimal d = 2.900m;
           Console.WriteLine("d = " + d);               // displays d = 2.900
       }
   }
   ```

   Le résultat de l’opérateur de concaténation de chaîne est une chaîne qui se compose des caractères de l’opérande gauche suivi par les caractères de l’opérande de droite. L’opérateur de concaténation de chaîne ne retourne jamais un `null` valeur. <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1995">Un `System.OutOfMemoryException` peut être levée si n’est pas suffisamment de mémoire disponible pour l’allocation de la chaîne résultante.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1995">A `System.OutOfMemoryException` may be thrown if there is not enough memory available to allocate the resulting string.</span></span>

*  <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1996">Combinaison de délégués.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1996">Delegate combination.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1997">Chaque type délégué fournit implicitement l’opérateur prédéfini suivant, où `D` est le type délégué :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1997">Every delegate type implicitly provides the following predefined operator, where `D` is the delegate type:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   D operator +(D x, D y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1998">Le fichier binaire `+` opérateur effectue la combinaison de délégués lorsque les deux opérandes sont d’un type délégué `D`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1998">The binary `+` operator performs delegate combination when both operands are of some delegate type `D`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-1999">(Si les opérandes sont de types délégués différents, une erreur au moment de la liaison se produit.) Si le premier opérande est `null`, le résultat de l’opération est la valeur du deuxième opérande (même si c’est également `null`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-1999">(If the operands have different delegate types, a binding-time error occurs.) If the first operand is `null`, the result of the operation is the value of the second operand (even if that is also `null`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-2000">Sinon, si le second opérande est `null`, le résultat de l’opération est la valeur du premier opérande.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-2000">Otherwise, if the second operand is `null`, then the result of the operation is the value of the first operand.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-2001">Sinon, le résultat de l’opération est un nouvelle instance de délégué qui, lors de l’appelé, appelle le premier opérande et appelle ensuite le second opérande.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-2001">Otherwise, the result of the operation is a new delegate instance that, when invoked, invokes the first operand and then invokes the second operand.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-2002">Pour obtenir des exemples de combinaison de délégués, consultez [opérateur de soustraction](expressions.md#subtraction-operator) et [appel de délégué](delegates.md#delegate-invocation).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-2002">For examples of delegate combination, see [Subtraction operator](expressions.md#subtraction-operator) and [Delegate invocation](delegates.md#delegate-invocation).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-2003">Dans la mesure où `System.Delegate` n’est pas un type délégué, `operator`  `+` n’est pas défini pour elle.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-2003">Since `System.Delegate` is not a delegate type, `operator` `+` is not defined for it.</span></span>

### <a name="subtraction-operator"></a><span data-ttu-id="a9118-2004">Opérateur de soustraction</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-2004">Subtraction operator</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a9118-2005">Pour une opération du formulaire `x - y`, opérateur binaire de résolution de surcharge ([opérateur binaire de résolution de surcharge](expressions.md#binary-operator-overload-resolution)) est appliquée pour sélectionner l’implémentation d’un opérateur spécifique.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-2005">For an operation of the form `x - y`, binary operator overload resolution ([Binary operator overload resolution](expressions.md#binary-operator-overload-resolution)) is applied to select a specific operator implementation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a9118-2006">Les opérandes sont convertis en types de paramètres de l’opérateur sélectionné et le type du résultat est le type de retour de l’opérateur.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a9118-2006">The operands are converted to the parameter types of the selected operator, and the type of the result is the return type of the operator.</span></span>
